<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нуть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duplo</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дупло.html>дупло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dupló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дупло.html>дупла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дупло.html>ду́пла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дупло.html>ду́пел</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дупло.html>ду́пл</a></b>)

<ol><li>tree hollow</li>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пилотка.html>пило́тка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pilótka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурацкий.html>дура́цкий</a> (3065)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурак.html>дура́к</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">durák</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-цкий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ckij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурачить.html>дура́чить</a> (25828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***дуреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дуреть.html>дуре́ть</a> (29034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>дурь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">durʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуреть.html>дуре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">durétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одуреть.html>одуре́ть</a></b>)
</p>

***дурить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурить.html>дури́ть</a> (17472)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duriti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурить.html>дури́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">durítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to frolic, to play pranks, to be naughty</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to behave like a fool
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>дури</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne duri!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">don't be foolish!; don't make a fool of yourself!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be obstinate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fool
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дурить.html>дури́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голову</a> кому́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>durítʹ</b> golovu komú-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to confuse smb; mix smb up</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***дурно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>ду́рно</a> (11011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>дурно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">durnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>ду́рно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúrno</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ду́рно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ху́же</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ду́рно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дурне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl form-of lang-ru comparative-form-of origin-ду́рно" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:дурень.html>дурне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>badly <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in a bad manner</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>ду́рно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обращаться.html>обраща́ться</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>dúrno</b> obraščátʹsja (s)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to treat badly, ill-treat</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Predicative">Predicative</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>ду́рно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúrno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>one feels bad, ill, unwell
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>ду́рно</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mne <b>dúrno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">I feel bad; I feel sick</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>ду́рно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dúrno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>дурно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">durnój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

</ul></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>дурно́й</a> (2662)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*durьnъ</i>, equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>дурь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">durʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурной.html>дурно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">durnój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)дурне́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:дурень.html>дурне́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>foolish, stupid
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">glúpyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:умный.html>у́мный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">úmnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>bad
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плохой.html>плохо́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ploxój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хороший.html>хоро́ший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">xoróšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>ugly
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:некрасивый.html>некраси́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nekrasívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красивый.html>краси́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">krasívyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>reprehensible
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нехороший.html>нехоро́ший</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nexoróšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>

***дурь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>дурь</a> (9397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*durь</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>дурь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">durʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>ду́ри</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>ду́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дурь.html>ду́рей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> folly, foolishness, nonsense</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> marijuana; grass, pot</li></ol>

***дуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a> (4081)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From Late <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dǫti</i> from Early <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dъm-ti</i>, from the root of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dymъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">smoke</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>дым</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dym</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">damp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>дуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подуть.html>поду́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дунуть.html>ду́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нам</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Véter <b>dújet</b> nam v licó.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The wind is blowing into our faces.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be drafty
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>Здесь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́ет</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zdesʹ <b>dújet</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There is a draft here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to go quickly, to scamper
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дуть.html>ду́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отсюда.html>отсю́да</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">A nu <b>duj</b> otsjúda!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Off with you quickly!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>
<ul><li>(no equivalent)</li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуться.html>ду́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вдува́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vduvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вздува́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzduvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вздуваться.html>вздува́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vzduvátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***дух.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>дух</a> (604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*duxъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>дух</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>dux</a></span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>spirit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>ду́хе</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne v dúxe</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in a bad temper</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>mind</li>
<li>courage</li>
<li>ghost</li>
<li>breath</li>
<li>scent</li>
<li>rebel (especially in Afghanistan; from <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дух.html>душман</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dušman</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> new recruit, rookie who is sometimes abused by the longer serving soldiers</li></ol>
